Action Required:

FYI

i. Forwarded under separate cover is an issue of a
supposedly "literary" Cuban publication containing two shor
essays by the Salvadorian poet and writer Roque DALTON.
The first of these essays is dedicated to LIRING-3. The
interesting thing is that LIRING~3 was at that time imprisoned
in Guatemala. The essay may thus be viewed as a tribute to
“a suciviidag supporter of the cause."

t

soe Bf

2. Roque DALTON (201-215097) is, according to the files
of the Station, an agent of the Cuban Intelligence Service’
engaged in clandestine activities for the Communist Party of
El Salvador. DALTON spent some time in Czechoslovakia and is
now living in Cuba. He is the brother of Margarita DALTON |
(201-751261), whom the Cuban IS recruited to work in Mexico.
LIRING-3 rot to know DALTON in Havana in 19€2-63 and became
a close friend of his (see HMMA-32283, 19 June 1967). DALTON
at one point confided to LIRING-3 that he had been approached
by WOFIRM while incarcerated in El Salvador. ,

3. The Station is hoping that DALTON's essay is an |
indication that LIRING-3 is going to be viewed by the Cubans
in much better light after his incarceration in Guatemala. i
A report of LIRING-3's complete debriefing by ROWTON was
forwarded with HMMA-35904, 27 November ek

A PALMA
NW

José Lezama ‘Lima ||

La palma de in imane sobre eb rio.
La palma paso a paso, hacia mi, leyéndome,

Narciso mascado por la nicbla ascendente,
vuelven los dioses desvensorces, Orfeo

y Stephanophorophoro. a
EL indice depmestra, sefala la inflexible

Tlanura de ta aleve, demucntea,

JED indice demnestra ta carreta sobre un hilo,

Ja dingonal can cuerpo de cocodrilo

y cabeza de gavilin,

el anilla de oro en el tumor de Ia luna,

Tar mano se extends sobre la danura

de nieve, la palma de In mano 7 t
acompasa la boga del rio.

La carreta conduce un canoso

reloj de pared. Iearo con dos guadafias.

Saturno se come Jas alas de eora,

So extiende, demuestra, so deja leor,

Iearo, ya calle, nadando,

Habla con cl Resucitado sentado en el Iégamo,

EL vencido por et sol regresa con las estaciones

y ot que triunfa de la muerte se vuelve a morir,

Es un boder du de cebolla, manzana y amapolas,

El airs esti exprimido en et puna

que se cierra, el arador por Ja palma de la mano
deja el reminiscente batido y batihojas,

el deseo paliducho, la serpicnte, el doble
del comicnzo, el truchimén vindicativo,
efreuto que golpea en las narices,

La capota caida se mide por su sombra.
Icaro vencido y cl Resucitado vencedor,
el Resucitado esperando la muerte

y el Icaro eterno relator.

En su sanpre cl laberinto y cl torete
oscuro luchando con el tigre dormido.

Action Required: See paragraph 3.

1. Forwarded herewith is one copy each for Headquarters
and the Guatemala City Station of the report covering the .
debriefing by Wallace B. ROWTON of LIRING-3 on his imprisonment
in Guatemala. Identity A of ROWTON's report is a Guatemalan
rebel living in Mexico who, as addressees will remember. |
noctaontally chst Llwecis an cue ieg a lew days prior to his
departure for Guatemala with LIRING-3. This wound may have
convinced the Guatemalans that he had recently.been involved
in terrorist activities and may, in fact, have cost him his
life. Identity B of the same report is the n:phew of Identity F,
a Mexican Communist who was arrested on 19 September 1968 ;
during a student demonstration in Mexico City; he is still ‘in
jail. : 1

2. As this dispa.ch is being written, LIRING-3 has an
appointment to talk at length apout his experience in Guatemala
with the LIRING Station Chief, LiRING-10. The general idea:
is for LIRING-3 to go to PBRUMEN in the hore that he can bel
used to penetrate PBRUMEN-sponsored subversion efforts in Latin
America or become, at least for a time, a reporting source in
PDRUMEN. :

3. ROWTON and the undersigned are prepared to travel to
Guatemala to discuss the LIRING-3 case and its Guatemalan/FAR
implications whenever the Guatemala City Station, after
reviewing the availabie information, feels ready for such

discussion. Please advise. 4) i
